amznJQ.available('jQuery', function() {
    var $ = jQuery;
    (function(){
        $('#acsux-menu li:first').addClass('acsux-active');
          var appendString = '';
        appendString += "<li style='background:transparent url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/img14/kitchen/slideshow/kitchen-bonavita_sliderbb._V364872693_.png) no-repeat center top; vertical-align;'><a href='/dp/B005YQZNO8&ref_=acs_ux_hsb_4s_2_s_KD-CG-ADC-MAIN' ><span class='hide-text'>Bonavita Coffee Maker</span></a></li>";
        appendString += "<li style='background:transparent url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/kitchen/groverc/coffeemakers/melitta_slide._V341145368_.jpg) no-repeat center top; vertical-align;'><a href='/dp/B00EI7DPK8&ref_=acs_ux_hsb_4s_3_s_KD-CG-ADC-MAIN' ><span class='hide-text'>Melitta</span></a></li>";
        appendString += "<li style='background:transparent url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/kitchen/groverc/coffeemakers/cuisinart_slide._V352452990_.png) no-repeat center top; vertical-align;'><a href='/dp/B00005IBX9/ref=sa_cm_ss2_cuisinart&ref_=acs_ux_hsb_4s_4_s_KD-CG-ADC-MAIN' ><span class='hide-text'>Cuisinart Coffeemaker</span></a></li>";

        $('#acsux-hero').append(appendString);

        acsuxSlider = {
            identifier: 'acs_ux_hsb_4s_',
            numSlides: 4,
            currSlide: 1,
            slidePos:0,
            animSpeed: 500,
            startSlide : setInterval(function(){
                    acsuxSlider.autoSlide();
            }, 5000),
            stopSlide: function(){
                clearInterval(acsuxSlider.startSlide);
            },
            slide : function(target, pos, type){
                if(type != 'a'){
                 acsuxSlider.emitEvent(acsuxSlider.identifier + target + '_0_0_' + type);
                }
                $('#acsux-menu').find('li').removeClass('acsux-active');
                $('#acsux-slide-'+target).addClass('acsux-active');
                $('#acsux-hero-wrap').animate({
                        top: '-'+pos
                    }, acsuxSlider.animSpeed);

                acsuxSlider.currSlide = target;
                acsuxSlider.slidePos = pos;
            
            },
            autoSlide: function(){
                if(acsuxSlider.currSlide < acsuxSlider.numSlides){
                    acsuxSlider.currSlide++;
                    acsuxSlider.slidePos += 360;
                    acsuxSlider.slide(acsuxSlider.currSlide, acsuxSlider.slidePos, 'a');
                } else {
                    acsuxSlider.slide(1, 0, 'a');
                    acsuxSlider.currSlide = 1;
                }
            },
            emitEvent: function(id){
                if(window.ue) {
                    ue.log({'v':1,'r':id}, 'acsux-widgets');     
                }
            }
        };

        //emit load events for widget and first slide
        acsuxSlider.emitEvent(acsuxSlider.identifier + '0_0_0_a');
        acsuxSlider.emitEvent(acsuxSlider.identifier + '1_0_0_a');
        
        $('#acsux-hero').find('a').hover(function(){
              clearInterval(acsuxSlider.startSlide);
        },
        function(){
                acsuxSlider.startSlide = setInterval(function(){
                    acsuxSlider.autoSlide();
            }, 5000);
        });
        $('#acsux-menu').find('li').hover(function(){
            var slideTo = parseInt($(this).attr('data-id'));
            var slidePos = parseInt($(this).attr('data-pos'));
            $('#acsux-menu').find('li').removeClass('acsux-active');
            $('#acsux-slide-'+slideTo).addClass('acsux-active');
            var t = setTimeout(function(){
                acsuxSlider.slide(slideTo, slidePos, 'u');
            }, acsuxSlider.animSpeed);
            $(this).data('timeout', t);
            clearInterval(acsuxSlider.startSlide);
        }, 
        function(){
            clearTimeout($(this).data('timeout'));
            acsuxSlider.startSlide = setInterval(function(){
                    acsuxSlider.autoSlide();
            }, 5000);
        });
    })()
});
            
</script>

      function acrPopoverHover(e, h) {
        if(h) window.acrAsinHover = e;
        else if(window.acrAsinHover == e) window.acrAsinHover = null;
      }

  amznJQ.onReady('popover', function() {
    (function($) {
      if($.fn.acrPopover) return;
      var popoverConfig = {
        showOnHover:true,
        showCloseButton: true,
        width: null,
        location:'bottom',
        locationAlign:'left',
        locationOffset:[-20,0],
        paddingLeft: 15,
        paddingBottom: 5,
        paddingRight: 15,
        group: 'reviewsPopover',
        clone:false,
        hoverHideDelay:300
      };

      $.fn.acrPopover = function() {
          return this.each(function() {
            var $this = $(this);
            if(!$this.data('init') && typeof $this.amazonPopoverTrigger === 'function') {
              $this.data('init', 1);
              var getargs = $this.attr('getargs');
              var ajaxURL = '/gp/customer-reviews/common/du/displayHistoPopAjax.html?' +
                         '&ASIN=' + $this.attr('name') +
                         '&link=1' +
                         '&seeall=1' +
                         '&ref=' + $this.attr('ref') +
                         ((typeof getargs != 'undefined') ? ('&getargs=' + getargs) : '');
              var myConfig = $.extend(true, { destination: ajaxURL }, popoverConfig);
              $this.amazonPopoverTrigger(myConfig);

              var w = window.acrAsinHover;
              if(w && $(w).parents('.asinReviewsSummary').get(0) == this) {
                $this.trigger('mouseover.amzPopover');
                window.acrAsinHover = null;
              }
            }
        });
      };

      window.reviewHistPopoverConfig = popoverConfig;
      var jqInit = window.jQueryInitHistoPopovers = function(asin) {
        if (typeof $('.acr-popover[name=' + asin + ']').acrPopover === 'function') {
          $('.acr-popover[name=' + asin + ']').acrPopover();
        }
      };
      window.doInit_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;
      window.onAjaxUpdate_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;
      window.onCacheUpdate_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;
      window.onCacheUpdateReselect_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;

      amznJQ.onCompletion('amznJQ.criticalFeature', function() {
          setTimeout(function() { amznJQ.declareAvailable('acrPopover'); }, 10);
      });
    })(jQuery);
  });
  amznJQ.onReady('acrPopover', function() {
    jQuery('.acr-popover,#searchTemplate .asinReviewsSummary').each(function() {
      if (typeof jQuery(this).acrPopover === 'function') {
        jQuery(this).acrPopover();
      }
    });
  });

<h2>Drip Coffee Makers from Amazon.com</h2>
<p>A good cup of coffee helps make your morning complete, so it's important to have a drip coffee maker that you can rely on. Whether you are looking for a programmable coffeemaker, a thermal carafe, or a personal coffeemaker that brews one cup at a time, Amazon.com has what you are searching for. Choose from models maxed out with features, such as a built-in grinder or permanent filter, or opt for a basic coffee maker that does what you need without any fuss.</p>
<p>Looking for a drip coffee maker that can make enough for everyone in your family or all of your coworkers? We pride ourselves on offering coffee makers in a wide range of sizes to handle whatever group you have to serve. Twelve-cup coffee makers from Hamilton Beach and Cuisinart can keep a large party satisfied, while 8-cup and 4-cup coffee makers provide enough for a small group and don't leave you with unwanted leftover coffee.</p>
<p>If you want to keep your coffee fresh for longer, choose a thermal drip coffee maker from manufacturers such as Melitta or Bonavita. These models feature a metal carafe that retains heat, so you can keep going back for another hot cup again and again throughout the morning.</p>
<p>The smell of freshly brewed coffee can help you wake up, and that first sip gives you the jolt you need to get your day started. Whether you are making coffee for a crowd or just brewing up a cup to enjoy on your own, a drip coffee maker from Amazon.com can help you achieve that perfect cup of joe.</p>
